set logical-systems rr-2 routing-options autonomous-system 65000
set chassis fpc 0 pic 0 tunnel-services
set chassis network-services ip
set interfaces ge-0/0/0 description vMX-02_ge-0/0/0
set interfaces ge-0/0/0 flexible-vlan-tagging
set interfaces ge-0/0/0 mtu 9000
set interfaces ge-0/0/0 encapsulation flexible-ethernet-services
set interfaces ge-0/0/0 unit 0 family bridge interface-mode trunk
set interfaces ge-0/0/0 unit 0 family bridge vlan-id-list 1-1500
set interfaces ge-0/0/1 description vMX-02_ge-0/0/1
set interfaces ge-0/0/1 flexible-vlan-tagging
set interfaces ge-0/0/1 mtu 9000
set interfaces ge-0/0/1 encapsulation flexible-ethernet-services
set interfaces ge-0/0/1 unit 0 family bridge interface-mode trunk
set interfaces ge-0/0/1 unit 0 family bridge vlan-id-list 1-1500
set interfaces ge-0/0/2 description vMX02_ge-0/0/2
set interfaces ge-0/0/2 flexible-vlan-tagging
set interfaces ge-0/0/2 mtu 9000
set interfaces ge-0/0/2 encapsulation flexible-ethernet-services
set interfaces ge-0/0/2 unit 0 family bridge interface-mode trunk
set interfaces ge-0/0/2 unit 0 family bridge vlan-id-list 1-1500
set interfaces ge-0/0/3 description vmx5
set interfaces ge-0/0/3 flexible-vlan-tagging
set interfaces ge-0/0/3 encapsulation flexible-ethernet-services
set interfaces ge-0/0/3 unit 10 vlan-id 10
set interfaces ge-0/0/3 unit 10 family inet address 192.168.1.1/30
set interfaces fxp0 unit 0 family inet address 192.168.1.201/24
set routing-options router-id 10.0.0.1
set bridge-domains VLAN1-1500 vlan-id-list 1-1500
